тАШ рдЗрдиреНрджреНрд░рдВ рд╕реНрддрд╡’ рдЗрддреНрдпрд╖реНрдЯрд╛рджрд╢рд░реНрдЪрдВ рдкрдЮреНрдЪрдордВ рд╕реВрдХреНрддрдВ рд╡реИрд╢реНрд╡рд╛рдорд┐рддреНрд░рд╕реНрдп рд░реЗрдгреЛрд░рд╛рд░реНрд╖рдВ рддреНрд░реИрд╖реНрдЯреБрднрдореИрдиреНрджреНрд░рдореН ред рдЕрдиреБрдХреНрд░рд╛рдиреНрддрдВ рдЪ—- тАШ рдЗрдиреНрджреНрд░рдВ рд╕реНрддрд╡ рджреНрд╡реНрдпреВрдирд╛ рд░реЗрдгреБрдГ’ рдЗрддрд┐ ред рд╕реВрд░реНрдпрд╕реНрддреБрдиреНрдирд╛рдореНрдиреНрдпреЗрдХрд╛рд╣ рдЗрджрдВ рд╕реВрдХреНрддрдВ рдирд┐рд╖реНрдХреЗрд╡рд▓реНрдпрдирд┐рд╡рд┐рджреНрдзрд╛рдирдореН ред рд╕реВрддреНрд░рд┐рддрдВ рдЪ – тАШ рд╕реВрд░реНрдпрд╕реНрддреБрддрд╛ рдпрд╢рд╕реНрдХрд╛рдордГ рдкрд┐рдмрд╛ рд╕реЛрдордорднреАрдиреНрджреНрд░ рд╕реНрддрд╡реЗрддрд┐ рдордзреНрдпрдВрджрд┐рдирдГ’ (рдЖрд╢реНрд╡. рд╢реНрд░реМ. реп, рео) рдЗрддрд┐

Jamison Brereton

89 (915)
Indra
Reс╣Зu Vai┼Ыv─Бmitra
18 verses: triс╣гс╣нubh
The poetтАЩs patronymic links him to the Vi┼Ыv─Бmitra clan of the IIIrd Maс╣Зс╕Нala, and indeed the final verse (18) is the Vi┼Ыv─Бmitra refrain, found in many of the Indra hymns of III (III.30.22, etc.). The penultimate verse (17d) mentions the Vi┼Ыv─Бmitras, though that half-verse seems to have been borrowed from the Bharadv─Бjas (VI.25.9). The poet appears to take his legacy quite seriously, for the hymn strikes one as self-consciously old-fashioned, a well-crafted Indo-Iranian praise poem, celebrat
ing IndraтАЩs high cosmogonic deeds in carefully balanced rhetoric and beginning classically with the 1st-person subjunctive announcement тАЬI shall praise IndraтАЭ (├нndraс╣Г stav─Б). The poet has also inherited the verbal cleverness appropriate to a proper r╠ес╣гi: his similes and figures of speech are aptly deployed, and he knows how to mislead his audience and withhold information for surprise effect. This particu
lar skill is clearest in verse 5, which appears to continue the praise of Indra, until we encounter as the first word of the second hemistich so╠Бmaс╕е, the real subject of the verse.
In the second part of the hymn, beginning in verse 8, we encounter another theme dear to the Indo-Iranians: the punishment to be meted out to those who break or play false to their alliances or have no alliances at all. The word mitr├б тАЬalli ance, ally, deified Alliance,тАЭ alone or in compounds, appears seven times in verses 8тАУ15, and is, of course, an element of the poetтАЩs ancestral name. Indra is repeatedly urged to punish the transgressors on behalf of the gods whose task is to maintain the proper relationships among men, namely Mitra, Varuс╣Зa, and Aryaman (see vss. 8тАУ9). It is striking that, unlike in many Indra hymns, we donтАЩt simply call for IndraтАЩs aid in battle against whatever enemies oppose us; in this hymn our enemies are characterized as moral failures.
There is another way in which the poet appears to show his consciousness of his traditionтАФone that we might hesitantly call тАЬintertextuality.тАЭ In verse 14 the poet seems to be consciously citing, with some variation, the famous Indra-Vr╠еtra hymn I.32. He asks that after IndraтАЩs exercise of vengeance the enemies тАЬwill lieтАЭ in a certain way: pr╠еthivy─Б╠Б ─Бpr╠е╠Бg amuy─Б╠Б ┼Ы├бyante тАЬwill lie there . . . in the (same) way (as) the embracer of the earth.тАЭ It is difficult not to see this as a deliberate con
flation of two famous phrases describing Vr╠еtra from I.32: 5d . . .┼Ыayata upapr╠е╠Бk pr╠еthivy─Б╠Бс╕е тАЬwill lie as the embracer of the earthтАЭ and 8a . . . amuy─Б╠Б ┼Ы├бy─Бnam тАЬlying in that way.тАЭ This quotation and conflation of phrases from a particular, and no

doubt well-known, poem seem quite different from the standard formulaic varia tion of our traditional poets, and it is perhaps not surprising to encounter it in the Xth Maс╣Зс╕Нala, as the practice of traditional poetic composition was drawing to a close.

рд╣реЗ рд╕реНрддреЛрддрдГ рддреНрд╡рдВ рдиреГрддрдордВ рдиреЗрддреГрддрдордореН рдЗрдиреНрджреНрд░рдВ рд╕реНрддрд╡ рд╕реНрддреБрд╣рд┐ ред рдпрд╕реНрдп рдЗрдиреНрджреНрд░рд╕реНрдп рдорд╣реНрдирд╛ рдорд╣рддреНрддреНрд╡рдореН ред рд╡рд┐рднрдХреНрддрд┐ рд╡реНрдпрддреНрдпрдпрдГ ред рд░реЛрдЪрдирд╛ рдкрд░реЗрд╖рд╛рдВ рддреЗрдЬрд╛рдВрд╕рд┐ рд╡рд┐рдмрдмрд╛рдзреЗ рд╡рд┐рдмрд╛рдзрддреЗ ред рдЕрднрд┐рднрд╡рддреАрддреНрдпрд░реНрдердГ ред рд╡рд┐ рдЬреНрдордГ рдкреГрдерд┐рд╡реНрдпрд╛рд╢реНрдЪ рдЕрдиреНрддрд╛рдиреН рдкрд░реНрдпрдиреНрддрд╛рдирднрд┐рднрд╡рддрд┐ ред рдпрдГ рдЪреЗрдиреНрджреНрд░рдГ рдЪрд░реНрд╖рдгреАрдзреГрддреН рдордиреБрд╖реНрдпрд╛рдгрд╛рдВ рдзрд░реНрддрд╛ рд╕рд┐рдиреНрдзреБрднреНрдпрдГ рд╕рдореБрджреНрд░реЗрднреНрдпреЛрд╜рдкрд┐ рдорд╣рд┐рддреНрд╡рд╛ рдорд╣рддреНрддреНрд╡реЗрди рдкреНрд░ рд░рд┐рд░рд┐рдЪрд╛рдирдГ рдкреНрд░рд╡рд░реНрдзрдорд╛рдирд╢реНрдЪ рд╕рдиреН рд╡рд░реЛрднрд┐рдГ рддрдорд╕рд╛рдВ рд╡рд╛рд░рдХреИрд╕реНрддреЗрдЬреЛрднрд┐рдГ рдЖ рдкрдкреНрд░реМ рджреНрдпрд╛рд╡рд╛рдкреГрдерд┐рд╡реНрдпрд╛рд╡рд╛рдкреВрд░рдпрддрд┐ рее

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬPraise Indra, the chief leadere (of rites), whose glory surpasses the lustre (of others), and the ends ofthe earth; the sustainer of man, who exceeding the ocean in magnitude, fills (heaven and earth) with radiance.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

I shall praise Indra, the most manly, who by his greatness forced apart the realms of light, apart the ends of the earth,
who, maintaining their boundaries, filled (them) in their expanses,
projecting beyond the rivers in his greatness.

Griffith

I WILL extol the most heroic Indra who with his might forced earth and sky asunder;
Who hath filled all with width as man’s Upholder, surpassing floods and rivers in his greatness.

Geldner

Indra will ich preisen, den M├дnnlichsten, der durch seine Gr├╢├Яe die Himmelslichter, die Grenzen der Erde weggedr├дngt hat, der die Welt mit seiner Breite ausf├╝llt, der V├╢lkererhalter, der an Gr├╢├Яe ├╝ber die Str├╢me hinausreicht.

Grassmann

Den Indra preis’ ich, der durch seine Gr├╢sse bedr├дngt den Lichtraum und der Erde Enden, Als V├╢lkerhort in weitem Raum sie f├╝llend, an Gr├╢sse ragend ├╝ber alle Meere.

Elizarenkova

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬThe heroic Indra causes numerous rays of light revolve as a charioteer (effects the rotation of) thewheels of the chariot; he destroys by his radiance the black darkness like a restless active horse.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

(As) the sun (turns) around the wide expanses, Indra should cause to turn here, like chariot wheels,
the one [=the sun?] that like a busy surge never stands still. He has
smashed the black shades of darkness with his flaring.

Griffith

Surya is he: throughout the wide expanses shall Indra turn him, swift as car-wheels, hither,
Like a stream resting not but ever active he hath destroyed, with light, the blackhued darkness.

Geldner

Dieser Surya umkreist die weiten R├дume. Indra m├╢ge wie die Wagenr├дder ihn herdrehen, der wie ein emsiger Strom nie stillsteht. Er zerst├╢rte das schwarze Dunkel durch seinen Strahlenglanz.

Grassmann

Er liess die Sonne durch die weiten R├дume hinrollen, Indra, wie des Wagens R├дder; Wie einen Strom, der nimmer rastend wirket, das schwarze Dunkel schlug mit ihrem Licht er.

Elizarenkova

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬSing along with me a new song, unceasing, surpassing heaven and earth, to him who like the pс╣Ыс╣гс╣нha(praises), born at sacrifices, overcomes his enemies, Indra who desires no friend.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Chant to him in the same old way a new sacred formulation that never turns away, without equal on earth and in heavenтАФ
to Indra, who has distinguished the races of the stranger, like the
(straight and crooked) backs (of horses), and need not seek (further
for) a comrade.

Griffith

To him I sing a holy prayer, incessant new, matchless, common to the earth and heaven,
Who marks, as they were backs, all living creatures: ne’er doth he fail a friend, the noble Indra.

Geldner

Ihm will ich das gemeinsame Erbauungswort singen, das nicht vom rechten Weg abkommt, das auf Erden und im Himmel nicht seinesgleichen hat, das neue. Indra, der die Sippschaft des hohen Herrn gemustert hat wie die Pferder├╝cken, hat keinen zum Freund haben wollen.

Grassmann

Ich sing’ ihm achtsam nun das neue, sch├╢nste Gebet zugleich f├╝r Himmel und f├╝r Erde; Dem treuen Indra, der wie Bergesr├╝cken die Wesen schaut und nicht den Freund im Stich l├дsst.

Elizarenkova

рдЗрдиреНрджреНрд░рд╛рдп рдЗрдиреНрджреНрд░рд╛рд░реНрдердореН рдЕрдирд┐рд╢рд┐рддрд╕рд░реНрдЧрд╛рдГ рдЕрддрдиреВрдХреГрддрд╡рд┐рд╕рд░реНрдЧрд╛ рдЙрдкрд░реНрдпреБрдкрд░рд┐ рд╡рд░реНрддрдорд╛рдирд╛ рдпрд╛рдГ рдЧрд┐рд░рдГ рд╕реНрддреБрддрдпрдГ рддрд╛рднрд┐рд░реНрдЧреАрд░реНрднрд┐рдГ рд╕рдЧрд░рд╕реНрдп рдЕрдиреНрддрд░рд┐рдХреНрд╖рд╕реНрдп ред рд╕рдЧрд░рдВ рд╕рдореБрджреНрд░рдГ’ рдЗрддреНрдпрдиреНрддрд░рд┐рдХреНрд╖рдирд╛рдорд╕реБ рдкрд╛рдард╛рддреН ред рдмреБрдзреНрдирд╛рддреН рдкреНрд░рджреЗрд╢рд╛рддреН рдЕрдкрдГ рдЙрджрдХрд╛рдирд┐ рдкреНрд░реЗрд░рдпрдВ рдкреНрд░реЗрд░рдпрд╛рдирд┐ ред рдпрдГ рдЗрдиреНрджреНрд░рдГ рд╢рдЪреАрднрд┐рдГ рдХрд░реНрдорднрд┐рдГ рдкреГрдерд┐рд╡реАрдореН рдЙрдд рдЕрдкрд┐ рдЪ рджреНрдпрд╛рдВ рджрд┐рд╡рдВ рдЪрдХреНрд░рд┐рдпрд╛ рд░рдердЪрдХреНрд░рд╛рдгрд┐ рдЕрдХреНрд╖реЗрдгреЗрд╡ рдпрдерд╛ рд░рдерд╛рдХреНрд╖реЗрдг рддрджреНрд╡рддреН рд╡рд┐рд╖реНрд╡рдХреН рд╕рд░реНрд╡рддрдГ рддрд╕реНрддрдореНрдн рдЕрд╕реНрддрднреНрдирд╛рддреН рее

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬI will utter praises to Indra in unceasing flow, (I will send) waters from the depth of the firmament (tohim) who has fixed heaven and earth on both sides by his acts as the wheels of a chariot (are fixed) by the axle.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

For Indra I have raised my songs, (like) waters in restless surges from the depths of the sea,
for him who propped asunder earth and heaven with his powers, like wheels with an axle.

Griffith

I will send forth my songs in flow unceasing, like water from the ocean’s depth, to Indra.
Who to his car on both its sides securely hath fixed the earth and heaven as with an axle.

Geldner

Zu Indra treibe ich die Loblieder, die wie Gew├дsser in rastlosem Strome aus der Tiefe des Ozeans flie├Яen, der mit Kunst Himmel und Erde wie die R├дder durch die Achse auseinandergestemmt hat.

Grassmann

Dem Indra will ich Lieder nun ergiessen in stetem Strom, wie Wasser aus dem Meergrund; Der Erd’ und Himmel kr├дftig, wie zwei R├дder zu beiden Seiten durch die Achse, festhielt.

Elizarenkova

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬAppeasing wrath, striking quickly, intimidating foes, doer of great deeds, armed with weapons,possessing the stale residue, Soma nourishes all the Atasa woods, they oppose no impediments against Indra.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Soma: or, Indra

Jamison Brereton

He who provides battle fury in his drink, whose first impression is sharp, the boisterous, vehement one with his arrows, who possesses the
silvery drinkтАФ
Soma! All the bushes and trees have not deceived Indra as
near-equivalents (of soma).

Griffith

Rousing with draughts, the Shaker, rushing onward, impetuous, very strong, armed as with arrows
Is Soma; forest trees and all the bushes deceive not Indra with their offered likeness.

Geldner

Der Soma, in dem man sich grimmigen Mut antrinkt, dessen Anstich scharf ist, der brausende, heftige, Geschosse f├╝hrende, aus Trestern bereitete wiegt alle Str├дucher und B├дume auf. Nicht haben den Indra minderwertige Ersatzpflanzen t├дuschen k├╢nnen.

Grassmann

Der Muth erregt dem Trinker und Erquickung, der eifervoll, bewehrt mit Pfeilen vordringt, Der Soma braust durch B├╝sche und durch W├дlder; wo er ist, schaden Gegner nie dem Indra.

Elizarenkova

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬOf whom neither heaven and earth, nor the water, nor the firmament, nor the mountains (are theobstructions) for him doth the Soma exude, when his wrath reaching his enemies destroys the strong and breaksthe firm.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

(To him [=Indra]), of whom neither heaven and earth, nor the dry land, nor the midspace, nor the mountains (are the equal), soma has flowed. When his battle fury is being drawn forth, he cleaves the hard and
shatters the firm.

Griffith

Soma hath flowed to him whom naught can equal, the earth, the heavens, the firmament, the mountains,-
When heightened in his ire his indignation shatters the firm and breaks the strong in pieces.

Geldner

Dem weder Himmel und Erde, noch das trockene Land, noch die Luft und die Berge gewachsen sind, f├╝r ihn ist der Soma geflossen, wenn sein Grimm gesteigert das Harte zerbricht, das Feste zerschmettert.

Grassmann

Ihm rinnt der Soma, dem nicht Erd’ und Himmel, nicht W├╝ste, Luft, noch Felsen widerstehen, Wenn nun sein Zorn zu h├╢chstem Grimm sich steigernd das Feste bricht, und was da steht, zerschmettert.

Elizarenkova

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬ(Indra) slew Vс╣Ыtra as an axe (cuts down) a tree; he demolished the cities (of the foes), he dug out therivers; he shattered the cloud like a new pitcher; with his allies (the Maruts) he recovered the cattle.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

He smote Vr╠еtra, like an axe the trees. He shattered the fortresses. He dug channels as if for rivers.
He split the mountain, just like a new pot. Together with his own
yokemates, Indra made the cows his own.

Griffith

As an axe fells the tree so be slew Vrtra, brake down the strongholds and dug out the rivers.
He cleft the mountain like a new-made pitcher. Indra brought forth the kine with his Companions.

Geldner

Er erschlug den Vritra wie die Axt die B├дume, er brach die Burgen, er furchte gleichsam die Str├╢me. Er zerbrach den Berg wie einen neuen Krug, Indra trieb die K├╝he ein mit seinen Verb├╝ndeten.

Grassmann

Er schlug den Vritra, wie die Axt die B├дume, er brach die Burgen, bohrte Bahn den Str├╢men, Wie neuen Krug hat er zerschellt den Felsen, die K├╝he holte Indra mit den Freunden.

тАЬYou, Indra, who are wise, punish the guilt (of worshippers); you cut off their sins as a sword (cuts off)the limbs (of victims); (you cut off) the people who (ignorantly) injure the supporting (function) of Mitra, andVaruс╣Зa, (which is) as it were their close friend.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

ItтАЩs just you, Indra, who are the insightful requiter of debts. As a knife does joints, you cleave the crooked (ways of those)
who violate the ordinances of Mitra and Varuс╣Зa, as people violate a bound alliance.

Griffith

Wise art thou, Punisher of guilt, O Indra. The sword lops limbs, thou smitest down the sinner,
The men who injure, as it were a comrade, the lofty Law of Varuna and Mitra.

Geldner

Du Indra, warst da ein kluger Vergelter. Wie das Schlachtbeil die Gelenke, so zerhaust du die Falschheiten derer, die wider des Mitra und Varuna Gesetze fehlen wie Leute gegen einen verb├╝ndeten Freund.

Grassmann

Du, Indra, als der weise Schuld-Verfolger, zerhaust das Unrecht, wie das Schwert die Glieder, Der Menschen, die des Varuna und Mitra Gesetz verletzen, wie den Freund die B├╢sen.

Elizarenkova

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬIndra rules over heaven, Indra rules over earth, over the waters, and over the clouds; Indra rules overthe great and over the wise; Indra is to be invoked for the acquisition and preservation (of wealth).тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Indra is master of heaven and Indra of earth, Indra of the waters and Indra of the mountains,
Indra of the strong and Indra of the wise; Indra is to be called upon in peace and Indra in war.

Griffith

Indra is Sovran Lord of Earth and Heaven, Indra is Lord of waters and of mountains.
Indra is Lord of prosperers and sages Indra must be invoked in rest and effort.

Geldner

Indra ist Gebieter ├╝ber den Himmel, Indra ├╝ber die Erde, Indra ├╝ber die Gew├дsser, Indra ├╝ber die Berge, Indra ├╝ber die Gro├Яen, Indra ├╝ber die Weisen, Indra ist im Frieden und Indra auf der Kriegsfahrt anzurufen.

Grassmann

Indra beherrscht den Himmel und die Erde, die Wasser Indra, Indra auch die Berge, Die Starken Indra, Indra auch die Weisen; in Krieg und Frieden muss man Indra anflehn.

Elizarenkova

рдЗрдиреНрджреНрд░рдГ рдЕрдХреНрддреБрднреНрдпрдГ рд░рд╛рддреНрд░рд┐рднреНрдпрдГ рдкреНрд░ рд╡реГрдзрдГ рдкреНрд░рд╡реГрджреНрдзрдГ ред рдЕрд╣рднреНрдпрдГ рджрд┐рд╡рд╕реЗрднреНрдпреЛрд╜рдкрд┐ рдкреНрд░ рд╡реГрдзрдГ рдЕрдзрд┐рдХрдГ ред рдЕрдиреНрддрд░рд┐рдХреНрд╖рд╛рддреН рдЕрдкрд┐ рдкреНрд░рд╡реГрджреНрдзрдГред рд╕рдореБрджреНрд░рд╕реНрдп рдЕрдмреНрдзреЗрдГ рдзрд╛рд╕реЗрдГ рдзрд╛рд░рдХрд╛рддреНрд╕реНрдерд╛рдирд╛рджрдкрд┐ рдкреНрд░рд╡реГрджреНрдзрдГ ред рд╡рд╛рддрд╕реНрдп рд╡рд╛рдпреЛрдГ рдкреНрд░рдерд╕рдГ рдкреНрд░рдерд┐рдореНрдиреЛрд╜рдкрд┐ рдкреНрд░рд╡реГрджреНрдзрдГ ред рдЬреНрдордГ рдкреГрдерд┐рд╡реНрдпрд╛рдГ рдЕрдиреНрддрд╛рддреН рдкрд░реНрдпрдиреНрддрд╛рджрдкрд┐ рдкреНрд░рд╡реГрджреНрдзрдГ ред рд╕рд┐рдиреНрдзреБрднреНрдпрдГ рдирджреАрднреНрдпрд╢реНрдЪ рдкреНрд░ рд░рд┐рд░рд┐рдЪреЗ рдЕрддрд┐рд░рд┐рдЪреНрдпрддреЗ ред рдорд╣рд╛рдиреН рднрд╡рддреАрддреНрдпрд░реНрдердГ ред рдХреНрд╖рд┐рддрд┐рднреНрдпрдГ рдордиреБрд╖реНрдпреЗрднреНрдпреЛрд╜рдкрд┐ рдкреНрд░ рд░рд┐рд░рд┐рдЪреЗ рее

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬIndra is vaster than the nights, vaster than the days, vaster than the firmament or the receptacle of theocean, vaster than the wind, or space or the ends of the earth; Indra exceeds the rivers and mankind.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Indra, the strong, projects beyond the nights and beyond the days, beyond the midspace and beyond the wellspring of the sea,
beyond the spreading of the wind and beyond the end of the earth,
beyond the rivers and beyond the settlements.

Griffith

Vaster than days and nights, Giver of increase, vaster than firmament and flood of ocean,
Vaster than bounds of earth and wind’s extension, vaster than rivers and our lands is Indra.

Geldner

Indra reicht weiter als die N├дchte, Indra, der Erstarkte, reicht weiter als die Tage, weiter als das Luftreich, weiter als die Grenze der Erde, weiter als die Str├╢me, als die L├дnder.

Grassmann

Der Helfer Indra ├╝berragt die N├дchte, die Tage er, die Luft, den Sitz des Meeres, Des Windes Weite und der Erde Enden, er ├╝berragt die Fl├╝sse und die L├дnder.

Elizarenkova

English translation:

тАЬMay your unbroken weapon, Indra, proceed (against your foes), like the banner of the shining dawn,like a stone cast down from heaven, pierce those whose friendship is deceitful with your consumingloud-sounding (weapon).тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Like the beacon of the ever-blazing dawn, let your insatiable missile go rolling forth, Indra.
Like a stone being launched from heaven, pierce with your hottest
weapon those whose alliances are deceitful.

Griffith

Forward, as herald of refulgent Morning, let thine insatiate arrow fly, O Indra.
And pierce, as ’twere a stone launched forth from heaven, with hottest blaze the men who love deception.

рдпрджреНрд╡рд╛ - рд╕реНрд╡рд╛рдорд┐рддреНрд╡реЗрди рдЬрд╛рдпрдорд╛рдирдореН рдЗрдиреНрджреНрд░рдореН рдПрд╡реЗрдиреНрджреНрд░рдВ рднрдЬрдиреНрддреЗ ред рдЫрд╛рдиреНрджрд╕реЛ рд▓рд┐рдЩреН, ‘рднреГрдЮрд╛рдорд┐рддреН’ рдЗрддреНрдпрднреНрдпрд╛рд╕рд╕реНрдпреЗрддреНрд╡рдореН ред рд╕ рдЗрдиреНрджреНрд░ рдПрд╡рдореНрдорд╣рд╛рдкреНрд░рднрд╛рд╡рдГ рдЕрд╕реНрдорд╛рдХрдВ рдЧреНрд░рд╛рдордВ рд╕рд╛рдзрдпрддреНрд╡рд┐рддрд┐ рее

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬThe months attend upon Indra as soon as born, the forests attend upon him, the plural nts, themountains, the affectionate heaven and earth, and the waters (attend upon) him.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

The months gave way to (him), the trees gave way, the plants gave way, the mountains gave way;
the two world-halves eagerly gave way to Indra; the waters gave way to him as he was being born.

Griffith

Him, verily, the moons, the mountains followed, the tall trees followed and the plants and herbage.
Yearning with love both Worlds approached, the Waters waited on Indra when he first had being.

Keith

The months, the woods,
The plants, the mountains,
The earth and sky in longing,
The waters, followed Indra on his birth.

Geldner

Es ordneten sich die Tage, die Monate, es ordneten sich die B├дume, die Pflanzen, die Berge und willig die beiden Welth├дlften, die Gew├дsser dem Indra unter, als er geboren wurde.

Grassmann

Dem Indra gaben Monde nach und W├дlder, dem Indra die Gew├дchse und die Berge, Dem Indra Erd’ und Himmel, gern sich f├╝gend, die Wasser ihm, sobald er ward geboren.

Elizarenkova

English translation:

тАЬWhere was your (shaft) Indra, (which ought) to be hurled (against your enemies) when you did cleavethe r─Бkс╣гasas hastening to war, and when the Mitrakru lay on the ground there in confusion like cattle at theplace of immolation?тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Mitrakrus: perhaps a demon; those who treat their friends with cruelty

Jamison Brereton

When will vengeance be yours, Indra, such that you will rend the demonic power of the evil one, which besets (us),
and that those who bloody their allies will lie there like cows at
slaughter, in the same way as (Vr╠еtra), embracer of the earth?

Griffith

Where was the vengeful dart when thou, O Indra, clavest the demon ever beat on outrage?
When fiends lay there upon the ground extended like cattle in the place of immolation?

Geldner

Wann wird denn dieses Strafgericht von dir, Indra, ├╝ber den B├╢sen sein, da├Я du den heranschleichenden argen Geist zerhaust, da├Я die Treuverletzer wie Rinder auf der Schlachtbank nur so platt auf der Erde liegen werden?

Grassmann

Wann wird dein Eifer sich, o Indra, zeigen, dass du zerschl├дgst den Geist, der Unheil br├╝tet, Wenn dort zerstreut wie Rinder auf dem Schlachtraum die grause Bande auf der Erde daliegt?

Elizarenkova

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬMay those adversaries, Indra, who press upon us, fiercely opposing us, and assembled in numbers,be overwhelmed with thick darkness, and may the bright (days) and nights overpower them. hymn you, and disregarding all other worshippers, come to us with your protection.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Those who, seeking to rival us, have battered at us, being greatly arrogant and powerful, o IndraтАФ
let those without alliance (to us) keep company with blind darkness. The nights with their good lights should prevail over them.

Griffith

Those who are set in enmity against us, the Oganas, O Indra, waxen mighty,-
Let blinding darkness follow those our fbemen, while these shall have bright shining nights to light them.

Geldner

Die feindlich gesinnt wider uns ausgezogen sind, sich gar stark f├╝hlend, die Gewaltt├дtigen, o Indra, die Unfreunde sollen in der stockdunklen Finsternis stecken; die lichtsch├╢nen N├дchte sollen ├╝ber sie triumphieren.

Grassmann

Die Feinde, die verworfenen, o Indra, die m├дchtig trotzend unsre G├╝ter rauben, Sie sei’n mit blinder Finsterniss umgeben, des Tages Helle m├╢ge sie vernichten.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬMay we, the descendants of Vi┼Ыv─Бmitra, sincerely praising you, Indra,by day for your protection,obtain your protecting (favours), may we obtain your recent (favours).тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

In just this way, Indra, might we know your new favors that bring benefits. And with your help, Indra, might we Vi┼Ыv─Бmitras know this, as we sing just now at dawn.

рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдордореБрдирд┐ - рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдердГ

рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдерд╛рдиреНрд╡рдпрднрд╛рд╖рд╛рдГ - (рдЕрд╕реНрдорд┐рдиреН рднрд░реЗ) рдЗрд╕ рдЬреАрд╡рдирд╕рдВрдЧреНрд░рд╛рдо рдореЗрдВ (рд╡рд╛рдЬрд╕рд╛рддреМ) рдЕрдиреНрдирднреЛрдЧрдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрддрд┐ рдХреЗ рдирд┐рдорд┐рддреНрдд (рд╢реБрдирдВ рдордШрд╡рд╛рдирдВ рдиреГрддрдордореН) рд╕реБрдЦрдХрд░ рдзрдирд╡рд╛рд▓реЗ рд╕рд░реНрд╡реЛрдкрд░рд┐ рдирд╛рдпрдХ рдХреЛ рддрдерд╛ (рд╢реГрдгреНрд╡рдиреНрддрдореН-рдЙрдЧреНрд░рдореН) рд╕реБрдирдиреЗрд╡рд╛рд▓реЗ-рдкреНрд░рддрд╛рдкреА (рд╕рдорддреНрд╕реБ) рд╕рдВрдХрдЯрд╕реНрдерд▓реЛрдВ рдореЗрдВ (рд╡реГрддреНрд░рд╛рдгрд┐ рдШреНрдирдиреНрддрдореН) рдкрд╛рдкреЛрдВ рдХреЛ рдирд╖реНрдЯ рдХрд░рддреЗ рд╣реБрдП (рдзрдирд╛рдирд╛рдВ рд╕рдЮреНрдЬрд┐рддрдореН) рдзрдиреЛрдВ рдХреЗ рд╕рдореНрдпрдХреН рдЬрдп рдХреЗ рдирд┐рдорд┐рддреНрдд (рдЗрдиреНрджреНрд░рдореН) рдкрд░рдорд╛рддреНрдорд╛ рдХреЛ (рдКрддрдпреЗ рд╣реБрд╡реЗрдо) рд░рдХреНрд╖рд╛ рдХреЗ рд▓рд┐рдпреЗ рдЖрдордиреНрддреНрд░рд┐рдд рдХрд░рддреЗ рд╣реИрдВ реерезреорее

рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдордореБрдирд┐ - рднрд╛рд╡рд╛рд░реНрдердГ

рднрд╛рд╡рд╛рд░реНрдерднрд╛рд╖рд╛рдГ - рдЬреАрд╡рдирд╕рдВрдЧреНрд░рд╛рдо рдореЗрдВ рдЕрдиреНрдирднреЛрдЧрдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрддрд┐ рдХреА рдЖрд╡рд╢реНрдпрдХрддрд╛ рдХреЛ рдкреВрд░реА рдХрд░рдиреЗрд╡рд╛рд▓реЗ рдкреНрд░рд╕рд┐рджреНрдз рдирд╛рдпрдХ рдкреНрд░рддрд╛рдкреА рддрд╛рдкрдирд╛рд╢рдХ рдкрд░рдорд╛рддреНрдорд╛ рдХрд╛ рд╕реНрдорд░рдг рдХрд░рдирд╛ рдЪрд╛рд╣рд┐рдП реерезреорее

рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдордореБрдирд┐ - рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдердГ

рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдерд╛рдиреНрд╡рдпрднрд╛рд╖рд╛рдГ - (рдЕрд╕реНрдорд┐рдиреН рднрд░реЗ рд╡рд╛рдЬрд╕рд╛рддреМ) рдЕрд╕реНрдорд┐рдиреН рдЬреАрд╡рдирд╕рдВрдЧреНрд░рд╛рдореЗ рдЕрдиреНрдирднреЛрдЧрдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрддрдпреЗ (рд╢реБрдирдВ рдордШрд╡рд╛рдирдВ рдиреГрддрдордореН) рд╕реБрдЦрдХрд░рдВ рдзрдирд╡рдиреНрддрдВ рд╕рд░реНрд╡реЛрдкрд░рд┐рдирд╛рдпрдХрдВ рддрдерд╛ (рд╢реГрдгреНрд╡рдиреНрддрдореН-рдЙрдЧреНрд░рдореН) рд╢реНрд░реЛрддрд╛рд░рдВ рдкреНрд░рддрд╛рдкрд┐рдирдВ (рд╕рдорддреНрд╕реБ рд╡реГрддреНрд░рд╛рдгрд┐ рдШреНрдирдиреНрддрдореН) рд╕рдВрдХрдЯрд╕реНрдерд▓реЗрд╖реБ рдкрд╛рдкрд╛рдирд┐ рдирд╛рд╢рдпрдиреНрддрдВ (рдзрдирд╛рдирд╛рдВ-рд╕рдВрдЬрд┐рддрдореН) рдзрдирд╛рдирд╛рдВ рд╕рдореНрдпрдЧреН рдЬрдпрдирд┐рдорд┐рддреНрддрдВ (рдЗрдиреНрджреНрд░рдореН-рдКрддрдпреЗ рд╣реБрд╡реЗрдо) рдкрд░рдорд╛рддреНрдорд╛рдирдВ рд░рдХреНрд╖рдгрд╛рдпрд╛рд╣реНрд╡рд╛рдорд╣реЗ реерезреорее
